Default Action Execution (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:446-489)\\n\\n**Activation Behavior Chain Item Methods:**\\n\\n**LegacyPreActivationBehavior() (lines 446-453):**\\n- Called before listeners on elements that want activation behavior\\n- Allows elements to suppress default behavior or modify event state\\n\\n**ActivationBehavior() (lines 466-472):**\\n- Called after event listeners have been invoked (in system event group)\\n- For HTMLButtonElement (HTMLButtonElement.cpp:315-349): submits form if in form\\n- For HTMLInputElement (HTMLInputElement.cpp): varies by input type (checkbox toggles, radio selects, submit/reset submits)\\n- Copies `mItemFlags` and `mItemData` to visitor for element-specific processing\\n\\n**PostHandleEvent() (lines 483-489):**\\n- Final post-processing for each chain item\\n- Allows elements to clean up or perform final actions\\n\\n### 8. System Event Group Dispatch (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:651-693)\\n\\n**System Group Handling:**\\n- First dispatches to default event group (content listeners)\\n- If event allows system group (line 652), resets propagation flags and retargets\\n- Calls callback if provided (line 671) - allows PresShell to handle default actions\\n- Re-runs entire dispatch chain for system group listeners\\n- System group is protected from content script interference\\n\\n### 9. Integration Points\\n\\n**PresShell Integration (layout/base/PresShell.cpp:9099-9101):**\\n- `PresShell::EventHandler::DispatchEvent()` bridges between widget system and DOM\\n- Converts native widget events to DOM events\\n- Provides default action handling through `EventDispatchingCallback`\\n\\n**Widget Events (widget/BasicEvents.h:637-875):**\\n- Core `WidgetEvent` class with message type, flags, and target information\\n- Flags control dispatch behavior: `mBubbles`, `mCancelable`, `mInCapturePhase`, etc.\\n- Methods: `DefaultPrevented()`, `PreventDefault()`, `StopPropagation()`\\n\\n**Event Messages (widget/EventMessageList.h):**\\n- Defines all event types: eMouseClick, eTouchStart, eKeyDown, etc.\\n- Organized by event class and category\\n\\n### Complete Event Lifecycle Summary\\n\\n1. **Creation**: WidgetEvent created with message type and target\\n2. **DOM Event Wrapper**: Created on demand from WidgetEvent\\n3. **Chain Building**: Walk DOM tree from target to root via GetEventTargetParent()\\n4. **Capture Phase**: Dispatch from root to target, capture listeners only\\n5. **Target Phase**: Dispatch to target element, both capture and bubble listeners\\n6. **Bubble Phase**: Dispatch from target parent to root, bubble listeners only\\n7. **System Group**: Repeat phases 4-6 for system listeners after default group\\n8. **Activation Behavior**: Execute default action (form submission, checkbox toggle, etc.)\\n9. **Post-Processing**: Element-specific cleanup via PostHandleEvent()\\n\\nThis architecture ensures complete separation between content and system events, proper event phase handling, shadow DOM support with retargeting, and clean default action execution following the DOM specification.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
